 This is the Indian team's first win in the tour of Australia, which started with a Test match played in Sydney on 26 December on the occasion of Boxing Day
 use isse pehle chaar maichon kii test shrinkhalaa main 0-4 se haar mili thi
 Australia won by 31 runs in the first Twenty20 match played at the Olympic Stadium in Sydney on Wednesday
 is tarah do maichon kii twanti-20 shrinkhalaa 1-1 se baraabar rahi
 Now the Indian team, led by Dhoni, has to take part in the tri-series in odis from February 5, in which Sri Lanka and Australia teams will also participate
 bharat kaa pehla match paanch farvari ko hi australia ke saath hona he
 In this match, the Indian team proved to be the host team in every respect
 gendbaaji ke dauraan jahaan usne australia ko 131 ranon par simit kiya vahiin ballebaajon ne badi aasaani se lakshya hasil kar liya
 With confidence, the Indian team has run out four batsmen of the host team, which is a positive aspect for the upcoming matches
 mejabaan team dwaara die gaye 132 ranon ke lakshya kaa peechha karte hue bharat ne acchhee shuruyaat kii or gambheer tathaa sahvaag ne pehle wicket ke liye 6
 43 runs in 3 overs
 sahvaag ne 16 gendon par do chauke or ek 104 meter lambaa chakka lagaakar team kaa iraadaa jataa diya
 After Sehwag's dismissal, Gambhir returned to rhythm and added a decisive 54 for the second wicket with Kohli
 kohli ne apni 24 gendon kii pari main teen chauke lagaae
 His wicket fell at a total of 97 runs
 iske baad dhoni khud ballebaaji ke liye aae or gambheer ke saath team ko vijay dilaakar hi laute

 finch ne 23 gendon par chah chauke lagaae

 The Indian players ran out four players while fielding brilliantly
 inamen se do ran out rabindra jadeja, ek-ek raina or rohit sharma ke naam rahaa
 Jadeja was adjudged Man of the Match for limiting Australia to a low score with two runs out and one wicket
 tippaniyan For India, Rahul Sharma and Praveen Kumar scored two successes each while Vinay Kumar and Jadeja got one wicket each
 praveen ne pari ke tisare over main david warner or shaan marsh ko out kiya tha

 finch, baile, dorthi or vade ran out hue
